Discovery and OpenAPI\n235: \n236: Apiservers serve the `/apis` discovery endpoints and the `/openapi/v2` and `/openapi/v3`\n237: specifications. The generation of the OpenAPI specification is a multi-stage process.\n238: \n239: *   **`openapi-gen`**: This tool reflects on Go structs, reads godoc comments, and looks at\n240:     validation struct tags to generate a map of all API definitions.\n241: *   **`zz_generated.openapi.go`**: The output is a large Go file containing a\n242:     `GetOpenAPIDefinitions` function.\n243: *   **Runtime**: The `GenericAPIServer` calls this generated function to build the final OpenAPI\n244:     JSON spec that it serves to clients.\n245: \n246: ## 7. Security & Observability\n247: \n248: *   **Audit (`pkg/audit`):** The apiserver has a policy-driven event logging pipeline.
